Content analysis is a research method used to systematically analyze the content of various forms of communication, such as text, audio, video, or images. Researchers use coding schedules or coding schemes to categorize and code specific elements or themes within the content being analyzed. This method is often employed in fields like communication studies, media studies, linguistics, and social sciences to examine and draw insights from textual or visual data.

Question 8
An approach to research in which the investigator creates an environment similar to one of interest in order to study behaviours in a realistic way, refers to: (UGC NET 24thMar 2023 Morning)
  • A.Naturalistic observation
  • B.Simulation
  • C.Longitudinal research
  • D.Correlational research
Correct Answer: Simulation

The approach to research known as "simulation" involves creating an environment or situation that closely resembles a real-life scenario of interest. Researchers do this to study behaviors, interactions, or outcomes in a controlled and replicable manner. This approach allows researchers to manipulate variables, observe responses, and draw conclusions about how individuals, systems, or processes might behave in real-life situations.

Question 9
Which of the following are advantages of quantitative interviewing over participant observation? (UGC NET 14thMar 2023 Evening)A. Wider range of issues can be discussed.B. Events can be re-constructed.C. Ethical aspects of research can be adhered to.D. Name-calling is permitted.E. Outsiders can be allowed to interrupt the process.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.A, B and C only
  • B.B, C and D only
  • C.C, Dand E only
  • D.A, D and E only
Correct Answer: A, B and C only

The advantages of quantitative interviewing over participant observation:

 

a. Wider range of issues can be discussed: Quantitative interviewing allows researchers to cover a wider range of issues through structured questions and standardized surveys. Researchers can design specific questionnaires that address various aspects of the research topic. This structured approach ensures that a broader set of topics can be explored efficiently and systematically.

 

b. Events can be re-constructed: While this statement is not listed as an advantage of quantitative interviewing, it refers to the characteristic of participant observation where researchers directly observe events and activities as they unfold. In participant observation, researchers can reconstruct events based on their direct observations. However, quantitative interviewing does not involve direct observation of events.

 

c. Ethical aspects of research can be adhered to: Quantitative interviewing often follows strict ethical guidelines and standards, ensuring that the research process adheres to ethical principles. Researchers can obtain informed consent from participants, protect their confidentiality, and maintain their privacy when using structured questionnaires. This ethical approach is crucial in research to protect the rights and well-being of participants.

Question 10
Given below are two statements (UGC NET 12thMar 2023 Evening)Statement I:The qualitative data analysis is governed by the codified prescriptions of quantitative data analysis.Statement II:Qualitative data analysis has many approaches, of which the grounded theory is important.In the light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:

  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.

  • D.Statement I is False but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Statement I is False but Statement II is true.

Statement I: This statement is false. Qualitative data analysis is distinct from quantitative data analysis and is not governed by the same codified prescriptions. Qualitative research involves the analysis of non-numeric data, often focusing on themes, patterns, and narratives, and it follows different methodologies and approaches compared to quantitative research.

 

Statement II: This statement is true. Qualitative data analysis encompasses various approaches and methods, and grounded theory is indeed one of the prominent and important approaches within qualitative research. Grounded theory is used for developing theories or explanations based on systematically gathered qualitative data.

Question 11
If research is done to find out behaviours and attitudes by analysing existing records and other materials, it is known as (UGC NET 02ndMar 2023 Evening)
  • A.Past research
  • B.Non-observational research
  • C.Non-participant research
  • D.Archival research
Correct Answer: Archival research

When research is conducted to find out behaviors and attitudes by analyzing existing records and other materials, it is known as Archival research. Archival research involves the examination and analysis of historical records, documents, artifacts, and other forms of existing data to gain insights into past behaviors, attitudes, and social phenomena.

Question 12
The panel study has the issue of (UGC NET 12thMar 2023 Evening)
  • A.Attrition
  • B.Single survey
  • C.Different variables
  • D.Inanimate objects
Correct Answer: Attrition

Attrition in a panel study refers to the loss of participants or respondents over time. In a panel study, the same individuals or units are surveyed or observed at multiple points in time to track changes or developments. However, attrition can occur when participants drop out of the study, which can introduce bias or affect the validity of the study's results. Researchers often need to address and account for attrition to maintain the integrity of panel data.

Question 13
Questions constructed in such a manner that suggest an expected answer are identified as: (UGC NET 11thMar 2023 Evening)
  • A.Main questions
  • B.Meta questions
  • C.Lead questions
  • D.Suggestive questions
Correct Answer: Lead questions

Lead questions are phrased in a way that guides or leads the respondent toward a particular response or perspective. They can influence the answers given by the respondent, potentially biasing the data collected. It is generally important in research and surveys to avoid using lead questions to maintain objectivity and collect unbiased responses.

Question 14
The post-test only control group design avoids: (UGC NET 11thMar 2023 Evening)
  • A.Non-Cooperative participants
  • B.Sensitization of participants
  • C.Group Comparison
  • D.Experimental treatment
Correct Answer: Sensitization of participants

In the post-test only control group design, participants are randomly assigned to either an experimental group or a control group. The experimental group receives the experimental treatment, while the control group does not. Both groups are then tested or assessed after the treatment. This design helps avoid sensitization of participants because they are not exposed to the pre-test, which can make them aware of the research hypotheses or influence their behavior.

Question 15
Given below are two statements: (UGC NET 05thMar 2023 Evening)Statement I:Non-parametric tests are not easy to use and are rather slow i.e., they require laborious computations.Statement II:Non-parametric tests do not suppose any particular distribution and the consequential assumptions.In light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Statement I is false but Statement II is true.

Statement I: This statement is false. Non-parametric tests are generally known for their simplicity and ease of use, especially when compared to parametric tests. They often do not require stringent assumptions about data distribution and can be applied to a wide range of data types. They are not typically considered slow or requiring laborious computations.

 

Statement II: This statement is true. Non-parametric tests do not assume a specific data distribution, making them more flexible and applicable to a variety of situations. They are used when data do not meet the assumptions of parametric tests, which often assume a normal distribution or other specific distribution.

Question 16
Given below are two statements: (UGC NET 01stMar 2023 Evening)Statement I:In Focus group discussions, the moderator is supposed to provide a liberal climate for participants to open up.Statement II:Participants of focus group discussions should rant individual experiences for comparison.In light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Statement I is true but Statement II is false.

Statement I is true. In focus group discussions, the role of the moderator is to create an open and non-judgmental environment that encourages participants to share their thoughts, opinions, and experiences freely. This helps in generating rich qualitative data.

 

Statement II is false. Participants in focus group discussions are not necessarily expected to "rant" individual experiences. Instead, they are encouraged to express their experiences, viewpoints, and perspectives in a structured and respectful manner. The goal is to gather diverse insights and opinions for comparison and analysis, not for participants to simply vent or complain.

Question 17
The photo-elicitation technique is used in (UGC NET 14thMar 2023 Evening)
  • A.Experimental research
  • B.Visual ethnography
  • C.Applied research
  • D.Content analysis
Correct Answer: Visual ethnography

Photo-elicitation is a research method commonly used in visual ethnography, qualitative research, and social sciences. It involves using photographs or visual images as a means of stimulating and facilitating discussion and eliciting participants' perspectives and insights on a particular topic or subject of study. Researchers may provide participants with photographs and then ask them questions or engage in discussions about the images, which can lead to richer qualitative data and a deeper understanding of participants' experiences and viewpoints. This technique is particularly useful when exploring complex or sensitive issues where visuals can help participants express their thoughts and feelings.

Question 18
What are the three types of auto-ethnography? (UGC NET 14thMar 2023 Morning)A. Unobserved talesB. Confessional talesC. Impressionist talesD. Critical talesE. Formatted tales.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.A, B and C only
  • B.B, C and D only
  • C.C, D and E only
  • D.A, D and E only
Correct Answer: B, C and D only

Auto-ethnography is a research method in which individuals reflect on their personal experiences and use these reflections to understand broader cultural or social phenomena. It involves combining elements of autobiography and ethnography to explore one's own experiences in the context of culture and society. Within auto-ethnography, there are several approaches or types of narratives:

 

a. Confessional tales: Confessional tales in auto-ethnography involve the researcher/authors openly sharing personal experiences, emotions, and self-reflections as a way to understand and critique social or cultural aspects. These narratives often involve candid and emotional storytelling, revealing personal vulnerabilities and experiences.

 

b. Impressionist tales: Impressionist tales use a more artistic or creative approach to convey experiences. They may include elements of fiction, poetry, or other creative forms to capture the essence of lived experiences. These narratives focus on creating impressions and evoke emotional responses from readers.

 

c. Critical tales: Critical tales in auto-ethnography involve a critical examination of personal experiences within the broader social and cultural context. Researchers/authors use their personal narratives as a platform to analyze and critique societal norms, power structures, and social issues. These narratives often aim to challenge existing norms and provoke critical thinking.

Question 19
Given below are two statements: (22 Oct 2022 Evening)Statement I:Visual ethnnography as a recent branch of research is dependent upon photo-elicitation to a large extent.Statement II:The visual research has not helped in empowering the marginalised people.In the light of the above statements. choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Statement I is true but Statement II is false.

Statement I: This statement is true. Visual ethnography is an approach to research that involves using visual methods, such as photography, videos, or other visual media, as a primary mode of data collection and analysis. Photo-elicitation is a technique commonly used in visual ethnography where participants are asked to take or provide photographs as a way to stimulate discussions and provide deeper insights into their experiences, perspectives, and cultural practices.

 

Statement II: This statement is false. Visual research, including visual ethnography, has demonstrated the potential to empower marginalized communities and individuals. By giving voice and visibility to marginalized groups, visual research can raise awareness about their experiences, struggles, and strengths. Visual methods can provide a platform for marginalized communities to share their stories and perspectives, challenge stereotypes, and advocate for social change. Visual research has been used effectively to document social injustices, highlight the lived experiences of marginalized people, and foster a sense of agency and empowerment within these communities.

Question 20
An analysis of the subjects life for meaning has the focus of: (10 Oct 2022 Evening)
  • A.Structuralism
  • B.Pragmatism
  • C.Sociology
  • D.Phenomenology
Correct Answer: Phenomenology

Phenomenology is a philosophical and research approach that focuses on understanding the meaning and essence of subjective experiences as perceived and interpreted by individuals. It involves an in-depth analysis of the lived experiences of individuals to uncover the underlying structures and meanings that shape their perceptions and actions.

 

An analysis of the subject's life for meaning aligns with the core principles of phenomenology, where researchers seek to explore and describe the subjective experiences and consciousness of individuals. Phenomenological research aims to understand how individuals make sense of their world and the meaning they attribute to their experiences.

 

On the other hand, other options are:

(A) Structuralism: Structuralism is a theoretical framework that emerged in linguistics, anthropology, and psychology. It focuses on analyzing the underlying structures and systems that shape human behavior, cognition, and culture. Structuralism seeks to uncover the deep structures that govern language, thought, and social practices. It is concerned with identifying the underlying rules, patterns, and relationships that define human experiences and behaviors. However, it is not directly related to the analysis of an individual's life for meaning, which is more aligned with phenomenology.

 

(B) Pragmatism: Pragmatism is a philosophical approach that emphasizes the practical consequences of ideas and actions. It focuses on the usefulness and efficacy of beliefs and theories in guiding human conduct and problem-solving. Pragmatists believe that the truth of a theory or idea is determined by its practical application and the positive outcomes it produces. While pragmatism is concerned with practicality and the real-world application of ideas, it is not specifically related to the deep analysis of an individual's life for meaning, as seen in phenomenology.

 

(C) Sociology: Sociology is a social science discipline that studies society, social institutions, and social behavior. It explores how individuals interact within social structures, how societies are formed and maintained, and how social processes influence human behavior. While sociology may touch upon the analysis of individuals' lives within the broader social context, it does not have the specific focus on understanding the subjective meaning and experiences of individuals that phenomenology emphasizes.

Question 21
When we separate social phenomena from social actors, it is known as: (23 Oct 2022 Morning)
  • A.Positivism
  • B.Relativism
  • C.Subjectivism
  • D.Objectivism
Correct Answer: Objectivism

Objectivism is an epistemological position that seeks to separate social phenomena from the subjective perspectives of social actors. It suggests that social phenomena can be studied and understood independently of individual beliefs, feelings, or interpretations. Objectivists aim for an objective and value-free approach to research, emphasizing the use of empirical evidence and scientific methods to study social phenomena. It is often associated with the positivist paradigm, which seeks to establish causal relationships and general laws through systematic observation and measurement.

Question 22
Subliminal priming as a research concept was first used in the discipline of: (12 July 2022 Evening)
  • A.Sociology
  • B.Political Science
  • C.Economics
  • D.Social Psychology
Correct Answer: Social Psychology

Subliminal priming refers to the presentation of stimuli below the threshold of conscious awareness to influence subsequent thoughts, feelings, or behaviors. In social psychology, researchers have used subliminal priming to study how subtle cues can influence people's attitudes, beliefs, and behaviors without their conscious awareness.

Question 23
Given below are two statements: (08 Oct 2022 Evening)Statement I:Triangulation is described as that of researchers taking different perspectives in answering research questions.Statement II:Triangulation is expected to produce knowledge from different insights to promote quality research.In the light of the above statements, choose the most appropriate answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are correct.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are incorrect.
  • C.Statement I is correct but Statement II is incorrect.
  • D.Statement I is incorrect but Statement II is correct.
Correct Answer: Both Statement I and Statement II are correct.

Statement I: Triangulation in research involves using multiple methods, data sources, or perspectives to study a research question. Instead of relying solely on one approach, researchers adopt different viewpoints to gain a more comprehensive understanding of the phenomenon under investigation. For example, if a researcher is studying the effectiveness of a new teaching method, they might use quantitative surveys to collect data from students, qualitative interviews with teachers, and classroom observations to get a well-rounded view of the topic.

 

Statement II: Triangulation is valued in research because it enhances the quality and validity of the findings. By using multiple sources of data or approaches, researchers can cross-check and validate their results, reducing the chance of bias or error. It allows researchers to identify patterns and consistencies in the data, increasing the confidence in the conclusions drawn from the research. Triangulation is a powerful tool to promote the credibility and rigor of research studies.

Question 24
A measurement based on properties of time, like minutes of a radio conversation is identified as: (21 Oct2022Evening)
  • A.Timeframe
  • B.Temporal unit
  • C.Timeline unit
  • D.Durational unit
Correct Answer: Temporal unit

A measurement based on properties of time, such as minutes, hours, days, etc., is referred to as a "temporal unit." Temporal units are used to quantify and measure time-related variables in research and data analysis. For example, if you are studying the duration of a radio conversation and you measure it in minutes, then minutes would be considered the temporal unit for that measurement.

Question 25
The measures of inter-coder reliability are employed in research related to: (09 July 2022 Morning)
  • A.Discourse analysis
  • B.Narrative analysis
  • C.Path analysis
  • D.Content analysis
Correct Answer: Content analysis

Content analysis is a research method used to systematically analyze and interpret the content of written, verbal, or visual communication. It involves coding and categorizing the content into specific themes or categories. Inter-coder reliability is used to assess the consistency or agreement between different coders or researchers who independently code the same data. This helps ensure the accuracy and validity of the content analysis results.

Question 26
Given below are two statements: (20 Oct2022Morning)Statement I:The panel design influences the statistical analysis in research.Statement II:The panel design does not suffer from the issue of mortality.In light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Statement I is true but Statement II is false.

Statement I is true because the panel design, also known as longitudinal design, involves studying the same group of individuals over an extended period of time. This design allows researchers to observe changes and trends over time and can have an impact on the statistical analysis.

 

Statement II is false because the panel design is susceptible to the issue of mortality, also known as attrition. Attrition occurs when participants drop out of the study over time, leading to a decrease in the sample size and potential bias in the results. This is a common concern in longitudinal studies, and researchers need to consider ways to address attrition to ensure the validity of their findings.

Question 27
Match List I with List II: (09 July 2022 Morning)List I (Types of Research)a. Cohort analysisb. Cultivation analysisc. Factor analysisd. Canonical analysisList II (Research Characteristic)(i) Study of a specific population as it undergoes change over time.(ii) Simultaneous analysis of two or more data tables.(iii) Analysis of perceptions of social world.(iv) A multivariate statistical test used for data reduction.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:Codes
  • A.a- i, b- ii, c- iii, d- iv
  • B.a- ii, b- iii, c- iv, d- i
  • C.a- iv, b- i, c- ii, d- iii
  • D.a- i, b- iii, c- iv, d- ii
Correct Answer: a- i, b- iii, c- iv, d- ii

Here is the correct matching of types of research and their characteristics:

 

a. Cohort analysis - (i) Study of a specific population as it undergoes change over time.

Cohort analysis is a type of research where a specific group of individuals, known as a cohort, is studied over a period of time to understand how their characteristics and behaviors change as they age or go through certain experiences.

 

b. Cultivation analysis - (iii) Analysis of perceptions of the social world.

Cultivation analysis is a type of research that focuses on how media exposure influences people's perceptions and beliefs about the social world. It examines the long-term effects of media consumption on individuals' views of reality.

 

c. Factor analysis - (iv) A multivariate statistical test used for data reduction.

Factor analysis is a statistical technique used to identify underlying factors or dimensions that explain the correlations among a set of observed variables. It is used for data reduction and helps in understanding the structure of the data.

 

d. Canonical analysis - (ii) Simultaneous analysis of two or more data tables.

Canonical analysis is a statistical method used to examine the relationship between two or more sets of variables. It helps in determining the linear combinations of variables that maximize the correlation between the sets.

Question 28
The domain of application in thematic analysis is: (10 Oct 2022 Morning)
  • A.Group comparison
  • B.Discourse revision
  • C.Text integration
  • D.Visual aesthetics
Correct Answer: Group comparison

Thematic analysis is often used to compare and identify patterns in groups of participants or different datasets. It involves analyzing qualitative data to identify common themes or patterns across the groups being studied, making "Group comparison" the appropriate domain of application for thematic analysis.

Question 29
In the deductive method, a researcher can begin his work with which of the following options? (23 Oct 2022 Evening)a. Policy statementsb. Social identity of the researcher.c. Theoretical postulations.d. Exploratory datae. By deriving a hypothesis.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.a, b and c only
  • B.a, d and e only
  • C.b, d and e only
  • D.c, d and e only
Correct Answer: c, d and e only

In the deductive method, the researcher begins with theoretical postulations and derives hypotheses based on existing theory.

 

a. Theoretical postulations: Theoretical postulations are the starting point for the deductive method. In this approach, researchers begin with existing theories, concepts, or models and derive specific hypotheses that can be tested through empirical research.

 

b. Exploratory data: Exploratory data analysis is not the starting point for the deductive method. Instead, it is a technique used in the initial stages of research to gain insights and identify patterns in the data, which can inform the development of new theories or hypotheses. In the deductive method, researchers start with existing theories, not with exploratory data.

 

c. By deriving a hypothesis: This is the correct option. In the deductive method, researchers begin by deriving specific hypotheses based on theoretical postulations or existing theories. These hypotheses are then tested through data collection and analysis to determine their validity.

Question 30
Given below are two statements: (11 July 2022 Morning)Statement I:In the inductive approach, a theory is generated out of research findings.Statement II:In the deductive approach, research is done in relation to the hypothesis drawn from the theory in question.In the light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Both Statement I and Statement II are true.

Statement I: In the inductive approach, a theory is generated out of research findings. This means that in the inductive method, researchers start with specific observations and data and then use them to develop general theories or concepts. They move from specific instances to broader generalizations.

 

Statement II: In the deductive approach, research is done in relation to the hypothesis drawn from the theory in question. In the deductive method, researchers start with existing theories or hypotheses and then collect data to test those hypotheses. They move from general theories to specific observations.

Question 31
Given below are two statements: (21 Oct2022Evening)Statement I:In content analysis, the researcher will code the text in terms of themes or subjects.Statement II:The categorisation of content is normally done according to the phenomena of interest.In the light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Both Statement I and Statement II are true.

Statement I: In content analysis, the researcher will code the text in terms of themes or subjects. Content analysis is a method used to systematically analyze textual, visual, or auditory data to identify themes, patterns, or meanings within the content. The researcher codes the data by categorizing it into different themes or subjects, which helps in analyzing the data in a structured and organized manner.

 

Statement II: The categorization of content is normally done according to the phenomena of interest. In content analysis, the categorization or coding of content is done based on the phenomena or topics of interest that the researcher wants to investigate. This categorization helps in identifying patterns or relationships related to the research questions.

Question 32
Which of the following are positive features of content analysis? (22 Oct 2022 Morning)a. It does not need sampling of contents.b. It is an unobtrusive Method.c. It is highly flexible in character.d. It is a transparent research method.e. There is no need to use it for longitudinal research.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.a, b, c only
  • B.b, c, d only
  • C.d, c, e only
  • D.a, d, e only
Correct Answer: b, c, d only

Positive features of content analysis include:

 

a. It is an unobtrusive method: Content analysis involves analyzing existing texts, documents, or media without directly influencing or interfering with the subjects or content being studied. It is non-intrusive and allows researchers to study materials in their natural context.

 

b. It is highly flexible in character: Content analysis can be adapted and applied to a wide range of materials, such as written texts, audio recordings, visual media, and online content. Researchers can use content analysis to study various types of data and gain insights into different research questions.

 

c. It is a transparent research method: Content analysis is transparent in the sense that it allows other researchers to examine and verify the analysis process. The coding schemes and methodologies used in content analysis can be made explicit and replicable, enhancing the credibility of the research.

Question 33
Match List I with List II: (23 Oct 2022 Morning)List I (Research concept)a. Hybridisationb. Epistemologyc. Iconic turnd. Yate's correctionList II (Description)i. Shifting from text to images as empirical material.ii. Used in Chi-Square test.iii. Moving away from a specific methodological affiliation.iv. Theory of knowledge.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.a- i, b- ii, c- iii, d- iv
  • B.a- iii, b- iv, c- i, d- ii
  • C.a- ii, b- iii, c- i, d- iv
  • D.a- iv, b- i, c- iii, d- ii
Correct Answer: a- iii, b- iv, c- i, d- ii

The correct matching is as follows:

 

a. Hybridisation - This refers to the blending or integration of different methodological approaches in research. Researchers may combine qualitative and quantitative methods, or draw from multiple theoretical frameworks to better understand a phenomenon. Hybridisation allows researchers to take advantage of the strengths of different methods and theories to enhance the overall rigor and validity of their research.

 

b. Epistemology - Epistemology is the branch of philosophy that deals with the theory of knowledge. It is concerned with questions about how knowledge is acquired, what counts as valid knowledge, and how we can justify our beliefs. In research, epistemology influences the researcher's approach to understanding reality, the role of subjectivity, and the methods used to investigate the world.

 

c. Iconic turn - The iconic turn refers to a shift in research practices from relying primarily on text-based data to incorporating visual and image-based data as empirical material. This shift recognizes the importance of images and visual representation in contemporary culture and the need to consider visual data in social research.

 

d. Yates's correction - Yates's correction is a statistical adjustment used in the chi-square test. It is applied when dealing with small sample sizes to improve the accuracy of the test. The correction compensates for the potential bias introduced when using the chi-square test with small sample data.

Question 34
Which of the following are advantages of content analysis? It is a: (14 Oct 2022 Evening)a. Transparent research methodb. Non-reactive methodc. Flexible methodd. Method that does not need a coding manual.e. Method that is free of any kind of framework.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.a, b and c only
  • B.b, c and d only
  • C.c, d and e only
  • D.a, d and e only
Correct Answer: a, b and c only

The advantages of content analysis are as follows:

 

a. Transparent research method - Content analysis is considered a transparent research method because it allows other researchers to clearly see and understand the process of analyzing and interpreting data. The steps involved in content analysis are generally explicit and can be easily replicated, making the research process transparent and open to scrutiny.

 

b. Non-reactive method - Content analysis is a non-reactive research method, meaning it does not require direct interaction with the subjects of the study. Researchers analyze existing texts, documents, or media content without directly influencing or interacting with the individuals who produced the content. This reduces the potential for bias introduced by researcher-participant interactions.

 

c. Flexible method - Content analysis is flexible in nature, allowing researchers to adapt and apply it to various types of textual or media content. It can be used to study a wide range of materials, such as written text, audio recordings, video clips, images, and social media posts. Its adaptability makes it suitable for diverse research contexts.

Question 35
Match List I with List II: (12 July 2022 Evening)List I (Type of analysis)a. Path analysisb. Content analysisc. Canonical correlational analysisd. Discourse analysisList II (Description)(i) Looks at argumentation systematically.(ii) Simultaneous analysis of two sets of variables.(iii) Represented by structured linear regression equations.(iv) Uses the method of unitisation.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:Codes
  • A.a- i, b- ii, c- iii, d- iv
  • B.a- iv, b- i, c- ii, d- iii
  • C.a- iii, b- iv, c- ii, d- i
  • D.a- ii, b- iii, c- iv, d- i
Correct Answer: a- iii, b- iv, c- ii, d- i

The correct match between List I and List II is as follows:

 

a. Path analysis: Path analysis is a statistical technique used to examine the relationships between multiple variables. It is represented by structured linear regression equations, and it allows researchers to test direct and indirect effects of variables on one another in a theoretical model. Path analysis is often used in social sciences to study complex causal relationships among variables.

 

b. Content analysis: Content analysis is a research method used to systematically analyze and interpret the content of qualitative data, such as text, audio, video, images, etc. It involves the process of unitization, where the data is divided into meaningful units, and then these units are coded according to predefined categories or themes. Content analysis is commonly used to study the presence of certain themes or patterns within a large body of data.

 

c. Canonical correlational analysis: Canonical correlational analysis is a multivariate statistical technique used to examine the relationships between two sets of variables. It helps to identify and understand the underlying structure that connects the two sets of variables. This analysis is used when there are multiple dependent and independent variables, and it aims to find linear combinations of these variables that show the highest correlation between the two sets.

 

d. Discourse analysis: Discourse analysis is a method used to study language in its social context. It involves the systematic analysis of texts, conversations, or other forms of communication to understand how language is used to create meaning and construct social realities. Discourse analysis focuses on the structure of communication and the ways in which language reflects and shapes social practices and ideologies. It looks at argumentation systematically to reveal patterns and underlying meanings in discourse.

Question 36
Focus groups as a technique is especially valuable in which of the following scenarios? (04 Jan Evening 2022)a. When the researcher has perfect clarity about the research.b. For obtaining general background about the topic or issue.c. For interpreting previously obtained quantitative results.d. When the researcher is interested in establishing a causal relationship between two variables.e. For generating a level of understanding about influences in the participants' world.Choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.a, b and d only
  • B.b, c and e only
  • C.b, d and e only
  • D.c, d and e only
Correct Answer: b, c and e only

Focus groups are especially valuable in the following scenarios:

 

a. For obtaining general background about the topic or issue: Focus groups are useful for gaining insights into participants' attitudes, beliefs, and experiences related to a particular topic or issue. They provide a rich source of qualitative data that can help researchers understand the underlying factors and perspectives of the participants.

 

b. For interpreting previously obtained quantitative results: Focus groups can be used to complement quantitative research findings. They allow researchers to explore the reasons behind the quantitative results and gain a deeper understanding of the participants' perspectives and experiences.

 

c. For generating a level of understanding about influences in the participants' world: Focus groups are beneficial for exploring the social and cultural influences that shape participants' perceptions and behaviors. They provide a platform for participants to discuss their views and experiences in a group setting, which can reveal shared norms, values, and attitudes within the group.

Question 37
Given below are two statements: (11 July 2022 Evening)Statement I:Multivariate studies demand larger samples than univariate studies.Statement II:Multivariate studies do not analyse the data sets involving several responses.In the light of the above statements, choose the correct answer from the options given below:
  • A.Both Statement I and Statement II are true.
  • B.Both Statement I and Statement II are false.
  • C.Statement I is true but Statement II is false.
  • D.Statement I is false but Statement II is true.
Correct Answer: Statement I is true but Statement II is false.

Statement I: This statement is true. In multivariate studies, researchers analyze the relationships between multiple variables simultaneously. Analyzing multiple variables requires more data points to ensure sufficient statistical power and to account for the complexity of the relationships between the variables. Therefore, larger samples are often needed in multivariate studies compared to univariate studies that focus on a single variable.

 

Statement II: This statement is false. Multivariate studies specifically deal with data sets involving multiple responses or variables. These studies aim to understand how different variables interact and influence each other. Multivariate analysis techniques, such as multiple regression, factor analysis, and structural equation modeling, are used to analyze such data sets.

Question 38
Retrospective studies are related to: (12 July 2022 Evening)
  • A.Social issues
  • B.Language development
  • C.Political events
  • D.Biographical research
Correct Answer: Biographical research

Retrospective studies are a type of research design in which researchers examine past events or behaviors to investigate their effects on present outcomes or to understand patterns over time. Biographical research is a common application of retrospective studies, where researchers study the life history, experiences, and events of individuals to gain insights into their development, behavior, and influences on their current state. These studies are particularly useful when studying the life trajectories, experiences, and contributions of individuals in various fields, such as history, psychology, sociology, and education.

Question 39
The research approach of hermeneutics is concerned with: (21 Oct2022Evening)
  • A.Textuality
  • B.Evaluation
  • C.Discourse
  • D.Interpretation
Correct Answer: Interpretation

The research approach of hermeneutics is concerned with interpretation. Hermeneutics is a methodological and philosophical approach to understanding and interpreting texts, symbols, and meanings. It is commonly used in fields such as literature, theology, philosophy, and social sciences to delve into the deeper meanings and interpretations of texts, language, and cultural expressions. Hermeneutic researchers focus on understanding the context, historical background, and cultural influences that shape the meaning of the subject under study. They emphasize the subjective interpretation of meanings and seek to uncover multiple layers of significance in the subject of analysis.

Question 40
A trend study is usually: (23 Oct 2022 Morning)
  • A.Action-oriented
  • B.Impression-oriented
  • C.Description-oriented
  • D.Experiment-oriented
Correct Answer: Description-oriented

A trend study is typically description-oriented. It aims to observe and describe changes or patterns in a particular phenomenon over time. Trend studies focus on identifying and analyzing trends, developments, and changes in variables or behaviors over a specified period.

Question 41
Match List I with List II: (12 July 2022 Morning)List I (Research method)a. Content analysisb. Social network analysisc. Semantic differentiald. Meta analysisList II (Characteristic)i. Summarisationii. Use of bipolar adjectives.iii. Focus on dyadic relations.iv. Context unitChoose the correct answer from the options given below:Codes
  • A.a- ii, b- iii, c- iv, d- i
  • B.a- iv, b- iii, c- ii, d- i
  • C.a- i, b- ii, c- iii, d- iv
  • D.a- iii, b- iv, c- i, d- ii
Correct Answer: a- iv, b- iii, c- ii, d- i

The correct match between List I and List II is as follows:

 

a. Content analysis - Context unit

Content analysis is a research method used to systematically analyze the content of various forms of communication, such as written texts, audio recordings, videos, etc. The context unit in content analysis refers to the specific elements or units of analysis within the content that are examined and coded. It could be words, phrases, sentences, paragraphs, or even larger sections, depending on the research objectives.

 

b. Social network analysis - Focus on dyadic relations

Social network analysis (SNA) is a method used to study social structures and relationships within a network. It focuses on examining the connections between individuals or entities, represented as nodes, and the relationships or interactions between them, represented as edges. Dyadic relations refer to interactions or relationships between pairs of individuals or nodes in the network, and social network analysis pays specific attention to these connections.

 

c. Semantic differential - Use of bipolar adjectives

The semantic differential is a research method used to measure the meaning or perceptions of a concept or object along a set of bipolar adjectives or scales. Respondents are asked to rate the concept or object on a series of opposing adjectives, such as good-bad, powerful-weak, happy-sad, etc. The use of bipolar adjectives helps capture the range of perceptions or attitudes towards the concept in a structured manner.

 

d. Meta-analysis - Summarisation

Meta-analysis is a statistical method used to combine and analyze the results from multiple independent studies on a specific research question or topic. It involves pooling data from different studies and performing statistical analyses to obtain an overall summary or effect size. The goal of meta-analysis is to provide a comprehensive and quantitative synthesis of the existing literature on the topic.
